All Emoji Families

See Also:Holding HandsIn LoveKissingHandshakesFlags

This page has every combination of family emoji. (53,424 Combinations)
Only Windows currently supports all of them. On other platforms they will look like their individual family members.
Most platforms also require a specific order for family members, so some will not work because of that.

ZWJ-Less Families

 These ones are gender-neutral and have the default 2 parents and 1 child.

Families with Babies

 Only Windows fully supports babies in their families.
